PERFORMANCE HALL\nNOV 28, 8:00 PM\nTickets: $55, $75, $100, $150\n\nLiza Minnelli followed her parents into the entertainment arena at the tender age of 2, co-starring with her mother in the 1949 film She is the only singer in history to sell out Carnegie Hall for three consecutive weeks.
